Metrics Collectors (`internal/metrics/`)\n64\t- **SystemCollector**: Collects CPU, memory, swap, disk I/O, and load averages using gopsutil\n65\t- **TokenCollector**: Parses Claude Code JSONL files to track token usage and costs\n66\t- **TmuxCollector**: Monitors tmux sessions and their status\n67\t\n68\t#### 2. Dashboard UI (`internal/ui/dashboard.go`)\n69\t- **Bubble Tea Model**: Implements the Model-View-Update pattern\n70\t- **Three Panel Layout**: System Resources, Token Usage, and Tmux Sessions\n71\t- **Responsive Design**: Adapts to terminal size with three layout modes\n72\t- **Auto-refresh**: Updates every 2 seconds automatically\n73\t\n74\t#### 3. Main Entry Point (`cmd/ccdash/main.go`)\n75\t- Command-line flag parsing (--version, --help)\n76\t- Terminal size validation\n77\t- Dashboard initialization and execution\n78\t\n79\t## Features\n80\t\n81\t### Layout Modes\n82\t1. **Ultra-wide (≥240 cols)**: 3 panels side-by-side\n83\t2. **Wide (120-239 cols, ≥30 lines)**: 2 panels top, 1 bottom\n84\t3. **Narrow (<120 cols)**: Panels stacked vertically\n85\t\n86\t### Keyboard Shortcuts\n87\t- `q` or `Ctrl+C` -
